    Task

    Explore Pricing Plans After a Free Trial Offer

    As a potential customer, I explore the pricing plans for Ahazou after considering a free trial, so that I can decide which subscription option best fits my needs for social media content.

    Success definition: Given I am on the Ahazou homepage and see the free trial offer When I click on the 'concordo' button to accept cookies and then click on the 'planos e preços' link Then I should be navigated to the pricing plans page for Ahazou where I can view various subscription options like Ahazou PRIME and Ahazou PRO, along with their features.

    Trajectory

    Step 1:

    Url (before/after):

    https://ahazou.com/

    https://ahazou.com/

    Reasoning for action: I reasoned that clicking on the 'planos e preços' link directly aligns with the user's goal of exploring pricing plans after considering a free trial. This action changes the webpage to display the specific plans available, thereby allowing access to the necessary information to compare and choose the preferred subscription option.

    Action: click(87) # Click on the 'planos e preços' link to explore the pricing plans.

    Change Description: After clicking on the 'planos e preços' link, the browser navigated to the pricing plans page for Ahazou. This updated the URL to 'https://ahazou.com/#planos' and displayed content related to various subscription options, including Ahazou PRIME and Ahazou PRO, with additional details and features related to each plan.
